  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_046bd0e1-359c-4637-9be8-a558893839a1'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

<div id="review_183825763" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/183825763" />
    <a title="Kitty" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5766810-kitty"><img alt="Kitty" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1553887580p2/5766810.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/183825763?book_show_action=true">Jul 10, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kitty" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kitty" href="/user/show/5766810-kitty">Kitty</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer183825763" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11511317285933286193">This series is the Harry Potter of cat books. I started reading these almost as a joke, but soon I was completely invested in this world. These cats were brought to life with personalities more vibrant and complex than many human characters. These stories are full of danger, friendship, forbidden love, betrayal, and self-discovery and it is all surprisingly believable for talking cats. I had physical reactions - crying, laughing, tightening in my chest - to this series. I would highly recommend </span>
  <span id="freeText11511317285933286193" style="display:none">This series is the Harry Potter of cat books. I started reading these almost as a joke, but soon I was completely invested in this world. These cats were brought to life with personalities more vibrant and complex than many human characters. These stories are full of danger, friendship, forbidden love, betrayal, and self-discovery and it is all surprisingly believable for talking cats. I had physical reactions - crying, laughing, tightening in my chest - to this series. I would highly recommend it, as long as you can suspend your disbelief, put away your preconceived notions about "talking animal books," and just enjoy a good story. No, it's not ground-breaking stuff, but it's beautiful in its own way. It left me staring at my cats and feeling vaguely disappointed that they couldn't talk.<br /><br />This one is my personal favorite, mainly because of the friendship between Fireheart and Graystripe.</span>
  <a data-text-id="11511317285933286193" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText5461508021209988218" style="display:none">I loved this book, I finished it in one day! It was amazing, and very exciting. In this book, Fireheart tries harder than ever to find out the truth about Redtail's death; and along the way, finds out that his best friend, Greystripe, is in love with Silverstream from RiverClan!<br />But being in love can be very dangerous for the Clan cats...<br />Even kits know that loving a cat from a different Clan is forrbidden. Most of the time, that love can cause big wars. <br />It almost does; becuase near the end of the book, Greystripe breaks the news to Fireheart: Silverstream is going to have kits! Now they <i>have</i> to tell Bluestar...when they do, RilverClan and ThunderClan decide to have a battle over which Clan is going to keep the kits. But lukcly, brave Greystripe breaks the ice by announcing that he will live with RiverClan; so the two Clan can avoid war, and Riverclan may keep the kits.<br />Will Fireheart ever see Greystripe again? <br />Read this awsome book to find out! I loved it!</span>

  <span id="freeText9508908522859887200" style="display:none">this book is about the old dark secrets in the 5 clans, Fireheart tries to get to the bottom of the mysterious deaths in the past, the truth he finds is unbelievable, and he finds other startling truths about the clans. He also find about traitorous plans in his own clan, he desperately tries to revile it to his clan, but his lack of authority brings him down,but time is running out. Every second the plan develops... there is also concealed love in the clans, but that comes to an end suddenly and unwarned. Fireheart gets a kin in the heart of winter but there is trouble in him with his enthusiasm. <br />I also really liked this book because the book is getting more interesting every second and it really urged me forward. Well again i really loved this book and the series and i hope to read on to the #4 of the warrior series!</span>
  <a data-text-id="9508908522859887200" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer158333671&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer158333671" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer12570744338255914075">After finishing the 3rd book in the first series, Forest of Secrets, I wish my local bookstore was still open this late so I could go buy the next book in the series! I am officially hooked, book 3 is action packed start to finish, with plenty of shocking twists and, as the title suggests, plenty of secrets, most of which are revealed by the end of the book, where everything....and I do mean everything changes. Fireheart is as usual, right in the middle of all this, struggling to do what is best</span>
  <span id="freeText12570744338255914075" style="display:none">After finishing the 3rd book in the first series, Forest of Secrets, I wish my local bookstore was still open this late so I could go buy the next book in the series! I am officially hooked, book 3 is action packed start to finish, with plenty of shocking twists and, as the title suggests, plenty of secrets, most of which are revealed by the end of the book, where everything....and I do mean everything changes. Fireheart is as usual, right in the middle of all this, struggling to do what is best for the clan &amp; his friends while desperately trying to discover the truth about his suspicions about Tigerclaw. Fans of the 1st two books should enjoy book 3 even more. I have to say I am amazed at how good these books are. The characters are surprisingly complex and engrossing &amp; their four-clan co-existence in the forest is richly detailed . That, coupled with the wildness of their surroundings make for an action packed plot. But where author Erin Hunter shines, is where she explores the themes of courage, and love and honor. Highly recommend book and series, I can't wait to see where the story will go from here!</span>

Still an engaging read. I regret not having read these books as a kid because I probably would have enjoyed them more because the characters are great and the idea and concept is intriguing.   <span id="freeText17759482105934826581" style="display:none">As the third book in the Warriors Series I found this story enjoyable. However, it was less solidified, less polished than the previous books. Still an engaging read. I regret not having read these books as a kid because I probably would have enjoyed them more because the characters are great and the idea and concept is intriguing. It's the overall composition of this particular book that detracts from its potential; it is a little jumbled, with various ideas and story lines interwoven sometimes unsuccessfully. Having said this, the ending had a fantastic spin. <br />3 stars. </span>

Could NOT put it down.<br/>Fireheart proves again and again his loyalty to ThunderClan and it`s leader Bluestar, but there are tragedies, broken hearts, deceipt and the enthusiasm of the younger generation in a hurry to be <br/>"grown up." Nothing new there, right. <br/><br/>Loved every word, from beginning to end. On to the next in this series: "Rising Storm."<br/><br/>Take it from me, you don`t have to be a child to enjoy these stories at all.</span>
  <span id="freeText10570117275268304257" style="display:none">Wow, finished that one in little more than 24 hours. Could NOT put it down.<br />Fireheart proves again and again his loyalty to ThunderClan and it`s leader Bluestar, but there are tragedies, broken hearts, deceipt and the enthusiasm of the younger generation in a hurry to be <br />"grown up." Nothing new there, right. <br /><br />Loved every word, from beginning to end. On to the next in this series: "Rising Storm."<br /><br />Take it from me, you don`t have to be a child to enjoy these stories at all.</span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2737161001" />

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessi (Novel Heartbeat)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessi (Novel Heartbeat)" href="/user/show/6759885-jessi-novel-heartbeat">Jessi (Novel Heartbeat)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780062366986" href="/book/show/22635873-forest-of-secrets">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6759885-jessi-novel-heartbeat?shelf=made-me-cry">made-me-cry</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6759885-jessi-novel-heartbeat?shelf=4-star">4-star</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2737161001" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16519300661468440090">Oh my god, this one broke my heart!! I didn't realize how invested I was, but this series has gotten under my skin. I mean, it IS about cats and we all know I'm a crazy cat lady. But to be honest I never expected to be this invested because I can't usually get into Middle Grade for the fact that it feels too juvenile. But, despite it being MG, this series is quite complex. It has it all - secrets, lies, betrayal, loyalty, leadership, love, friendship, and family value. Even death.<br/><br/>There were some</span>
  <span id="freeText16519300661468440090" style="display:none">Oh my god, this one broke my heart!! I didn't realize how invested I was, but this series has gotten under my skin. I mean, it IS about cats and we all know I'm a crazy cat lady. But to be honest I never expected to be this invested because I can't usually get into Middle Grade for the fact that it feels too juvenile. But, despite it being MG, this series is quite complex. It has it all - secrets, lies, betrayal, loyalty, leadership, love, friendship, and family value. Even death.<br /><br />There were some nice little twists in there, too - you could see them coming a mile away because of the giant hints dropped and some painfully obvious foreshadowing, but it still made for a great plot line. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[It was easy to guess that the lost ThunderClan kits belonged to Bluestar, and that Tigerclaw was bad news and was plotting with Brokentail. But I still enjoyed reading about it!<br /><br />I freaking cried when Silverstream died. I was shocked when she said she was going to have Graystripe's kits, and I never saw it coming that she would die during birthing. That part got me bad! I was also sobbing at the end when Graystripe decided to leave and join RiverClan with his kits. The loss of Fireheart's best friend and everything that entailed just broke my heart into little pieces! It reminded me of the end of The Fox and the Hound *sobs*<br /><br />I was also incredibly surprised to find that I was affected by Brokentail's death. He was horrible, yes, but I still cried. Mostly I was just upset on behalf of Yellowfang, because I love her and it was such a hard decision for her to make. That scene was so heartbreaking! Poor Yellowfang :(  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Basically, if you haven't read this series, you should! It's great for all ages!</span>
  <a data-text-id="16519300661468440090" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1098054863?book_show_action=true">Nov 05, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Charlie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Charlie" href="/user/show/36370903-charlie">Charlie</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1098054863" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15746024959565174340">This book was a pretty good book in the Warriors series. Forest of Secrets leaves you on a cliff hanger leaving you in a state of shock. I do believe this book had so many plotlines at some parts of the book, that it may leave a reader confused. I also believe that the plotline in this book was not so dissimilar from the previous books in the series. Forest Of Secrets is a likable book, but it is not one of those books that gives you the feeling that you can not put the book down because it capt</span>
  <span id="freeText15746024959565174340" style="display:none">This book was a pretty good book in the Warriors series. Forest of Secrets leaves you on a cliff hanger leaving you in a state of shock. I do believe this book had so many plotlines at some parts of the book, that it may leave a reader confused. I also believe that the plotline in this book was not so dissimilar from the previous books in the series. Forest Of Secrets is a likable book, but it is not one of those books that gives you the feeling that you can not put the book down because it captivates you so (Harry Potter Series). I started reading this series in 2013 but stopped at Book 2 because I did not find it was so enticing. I believe this series is definitely more for a juvenile reader; hence my discontinuation of reading the series. If you are above 12; I don't believe you will find it as interesting as a 9-10 year old. </span>

          </span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('xfdidHoSuWJ1Rn3mvF1KMWwBTN+/P7sY43MWY4j/9qikxXEU1V7TOxjFuiXTUTuK3+fkJBf94Olv0NLoCJ08jA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('AK7H8uG5KcJFAzS+cNeNtoyNSsuz/lv3pzaaQE3GExBhnNSSTvVDmyiA830f2/wNP2viMBs8AAYrlV7LzaTZNA==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer3665465597567518196">Erin Hunter is the pseudonym of five people: <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/132369.Kate_Cary' title='Kate Cary' rel='nofollow noopener'>Kate Cary</a>, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/220345.Cherith_Baldry' title='Cherith Baldry' rel='nofollow noopener'>Cherith Baldry</a>, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/374504.Tui_T__Sutherland' title='Tui T. Sutherland' rel='nofollow noopener'>Tui T. Sutherland</a>, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2742182.Gillian_Philip' title='Gillian Philip' rel='nofollow noopener'>Gillian Philip</a>, and <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/769868.Inbali_Iserles' title='Inbali Iserles' rel='nofollow noopener'>Inbali Iserles</a>, as well as editor <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/645010.Victoria_Holmes' title='Victoria Holmes' rel='nofollow noopener'>Victoria Holmes</a>. Together, they write the Warriors series as well as the Seekers and Survivors series. Erin Hunter is working on a new series now called Bravelands. <br/><br/>Erin Hunter is inspired by a love of cats and a fascination with the ferocity of the natur</span>
  <span id="freeText3665465597567518196" style="display:none">Erin Hunter is the pseudonym of five people: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/132369.Kate_Cary" title="Kate Cary" rel="nofollow noopener">Kate Cary</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/220345.Cherith_Baldry" title="Cherith Baldry" rel="nofollow noopener">Cherith Baldry</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/374504.Tui_T__Sutherland" title="Tui T. Sutherland" rel="nofollow noopener">Tui T. Sutherland</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2742182.Gillian_Philip" title="Gillian Philip" rel="nofollow noopener">Gillian Philip</a>, and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/769868.Inbali_Iserles" title="Inbali Iserles" rel="nofollow noopener">Inbali Iserles</a>, as well as editor <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/645010.Victoria_Holmes" title="Victoria Holmes" rel="nofollow noopener">Victoria Holmes</a>. Together, they write the Warriors series as well as the Seekers and Survivors series. Erin Hunter is working on a new series now called Bravelands. <br /><br />Erin Hunter is inspired by a love of cats and a fascination with the ferocity of the natural world. As well as having a great respect for nature in all its forms, Erin enjoys creating rich mythical explanations for animal behavior, shaped by her interest in astronomy and standing stones.</span>
